## v10.7.0

Released January 12, 2024

### Notable Changes

CSS property values are now pulled from Webref! This will let us easily add all supported CSS property values to BCD as they are implemented.

### Commits

- Fix unittests
- Add additional overrides
- Add additional custom tests
- Generate constructor tests even with `[HTMLConstructor]` ext-attr
- Add IDL for various features tracked in BCD but missing from collector
- Add overrides for notifications on Safari
- Add detached/transferToFixed to ArrayBuffer ([#1003](https://github.com/openwebdocs/mdn-bcd-collector/pull/1003))
- Ignore streamingCompilation in wasm-feature-detect ([#1002](https://github.com/openwebdocs/mdn-bcd-collector/pull/1002))
- Adds ability to check for possible updates across multiple default statements ([#967](https://github.com/openwebdocs/mdn-bcd-collector/pull/967))
- Replace SVG attribute names in custom/element.json ([#998](https://github.com/openwebdocs/mdn-bcd-collector/pull/998))
- Fix more HTML attribute reflection names ([#997](https://github.com/openwebdocs/mdn-bcd-collector/pull/997))
- Provide better tests for SVG attributes ([#990](https://github.com/openwebdocs/mdn-bcd-collector/pull/990))
- Makes output arg for feature-list.json more explicitly optional ([#995](https://github.com/openwebdocs/mdn-bcd-collector/pull/995))
- Add custom rule for `plus-darker`in mix-blend-mode ([#991](https://github.com/openwebdocs/mdn-bcd-collector/pull/991))
- Add ArrayBuffer.transfer ([#994](https://github.com/openwebdocs/mdn-bcd-collector/pull/994))
- Outputs a log of updated features ([#947](https://github.com/openwebdocs/mdn-bcd-collector/pull/947))

## v10.3.0

Released November 7, 2023

### Notable Changes

Originally, the JavaScript spec was manually scraped using https://github.com/jc-verse/mdn-checker every once in a while, as there was no NPM package available. Now, the relevant code has been obtained from the [es-scraper](https://github.com/jc-verse/mdn-checker/tree/master/packages/es-scraper) package in the repository and integrated directly into the JavaScript test generation. Once an NPM package version is available, we will switch to using the package instead.

### Commits

- Fix test for animate SVG element "dur" attribute
- Remove referrerPolcy attribute on SVG &lt;a&gt; element
- Fix tests for attributes with different property names
- Remove Firefox-proprietary attributes
- Fix tests for form\* attributes on button/input elements
- Simplify defining HTML/SVG attributes with different prop names
- Fix "bgcolor" attribute testing

## v10.0.0

Released June 13, 2023

### Notable changes

With this new collector release, a number of big updates have been implemented to greatly improve coverage of features within BCD. Three new categories have been added:

- HTML elements and attributes
- SVG elements and attributes
- WebAssembly features

The core for MathML elements is also implemented, but as MathML requires additional test code and cannot be tested the same way that HTML and SVG elements are tested, it has been disabled.
